/* === Batch 6 refinement (2026-05-17) -- cross-validate `tools/rename_funcs.py` === */
/* `tools/rename_funcs.py` ships a ~400-entry legacy rename map assembled from */
/* prior Kengo affinity / size-match research that was never propagated into */
/* `named_syms.txt`. The three entries below pass cross-validation against the */
/* current asm bodies; the rest of the file's 7 batch-6 'low' wrappers either */
/* (a) have legacy names that conflict with their body's named callees, or */
/* (b) lack callsite context to distinguish their role.  See */
/* `docs/naming/MISNOMERS.md` and `tools/rename_funcs.py` for the full delta. */

/* === Menu-control cluster at 0x800A34F8-3514 (2026-05-17) -- 4 highs === */
/* Discovered via cluster-consumer analysis: D_800A34F8/350C/3514 are */
/* the top "naming multiplier" cluster -- 6+ consumer functions all */
/* reference these together.  text1b.c:14910-15533 shows the pattern: */
/*   - D_800A34F8 is a packed bitfield with cycling sub-fields */
/*     (bits 0-3 = rotating slot index, bits 10-12 = sub-cursor, */
/*      bits 13-15 = main cursor position) */
/*   - D_800A34FC is a struct pointer assigned from func_8006E49C */
/*     (the mode-state allocator), accessed at offsets 0x12/0x10/0xE/ */
/*     0xC/0x28/0x2A/0x30 */
/*   - D_800A3514 is a pure frame counter (only += 1 or = 0) */
/*   - func_8006B92C is a menu input handler: parses pad input, */
/*     decodes direction (1=down, 2=up), navigates cursor, */
/*     calls func_8005C650 for menu sound effects */
g_menuctl_state_bitfield                                = 0x800A34F8;  /* packed cursor/slot state */
g_menuctl_mode_state_ptr                                = 0x800A34FC;  /* current screen's state struct pointer */
g_menuctl_pad_result_buf                                = 0x800A350C;  /* s16 pad-decode result base (4 entries: 350C/350E/3510/3512) */
g_menuctl_frame_counter                                 = 0x800A3514;  /* per-frame tick counter (reset to 0, += 1 each frame) */

/* === Effect/physics object cluster (2026-05-17) -- 4 highs === */
/* From text1b.c func_80053304 (line 11052) + func_8005344C (11082): */
/* D_800A33F4 is the active effect-state pointer; the struct it points */
/* to has a 96-byte layout with: */
/*   +0x8/+0xC/+0x10 = vx/vy/vz (current position) */
/*   +0x18/+0x1C/+0x20 = bx/by/bz (target/base position) */
/*   +0x5C = handler function pointer */
/* The flow: compute |b-v| via func_80052754, if <= 0x9C3F (40000) */
/* reflect v to opposite side of b and set handler = func_80053754; */
/* otherwise set handler = func_80053E9C. */
g_effect_active_ptr                                     = 0x800A33F4;  /* pointer to currently-active effect/physics state struct */
g_effect_struct_a                                       = 0x800EF9F8;  /* effect state struct base (assigned to g_effect_active_ptr in func_80053304) */
g_effect_struct_a_vfield                                = 0x800EFA00;  /* effect_struct_a + 8 (first vector field, vx) */
g_effect_struct_b                                       = 0x800EFC38;  /* second effect state struct (parallel to g_effect_struct_a) */
